class="circle-group_item" data-v-0a6f4daa data-v-0a6f4daa></circle></g></g></svg></div></div></div></section> <section class="section section-01" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="section__inner flex-container" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="block-text section-intro w-100 w-50-m" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="block-text__inner" data-v-0a6f4daa><h2 class="section-01-intro pa1 pt2" data-v-0a6f4daa>
              One Australian suffers a heart attack every nine minutes.
            </h2> <p class="section-01-intro__text pa1 caption_ts" data-v-0a6f4daa>
              Traditional risk factors such as smoking and diabetes help
              predict heart attacks. However, about 25% have developed silent
              coronary artery disease over years and have no risk factor
              “alarms”.
            </p></div></div></div></section> <section class="section section-02" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="section__inner flex-container" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="block-text section-intro w-100 w-50-m" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="block-text__inner" data-v-0a6f4daa><h2 class="section-02-intro pa1 pt2" data-v-0a6f4daa>
              That's 160 Australians suffering heart attacks every day
            </h2> <p class="section-02-intro__text pa1 caption_ts" data-v-0a6f4daa>
              Underpinning this is the need to discover new ways of detecting
              early coronary artery disease.
            </p></div></div></div></section> <section class="section section-03" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="section__inner flex-container" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="block-text section-intro w-100 w-50-m" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="block-text__inner" data-v-0a6f4daa><h2 class="section-03-intro pa1 pt2" data-v-0a6f4daa>
              We have a vision: moving towards zero heart attacks.
            </h2> <p class="section-03-intro__text pa1 caption_ts" data-v-0a6f4daa>
              If we can detect this plaque early, treatment can prevent
              progression and heart attacks are (almost) completely
              preventable. <br data-v-0a6f4daa><br data-v-0a6f4daa>Put simply, no plaque = no heart
              attack.
            </p></div></div></div></section> <section class="section section-04" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="section__inner flex-container" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="block-text section-intro w-100 w-50-m" data-v-0a6f4daa><div class="block-text__inner" data-v-0a6f4daa><h2 class="pa1 pt2" data-v-0a6f4daa>Our research</h2> <p class="pa1 pt2 caption_ts" data-v-0a6f4daa>
              CAD Frontiers is an Australian led, international team at the
              cutting edge of coronary artery disease research and clinical
              practice.<br data-v-0a6f4daa><br data-v-0a6f4daa>
              We’re driving innovation to transform heart attack prevention
              across three core research areas:
